Across four MultiBench benchmarks, S3 improves accuracy and shows a consistent reverse U-shaped sparsity-performance trend, with peak performance at intermediate sparsity. Method: 将基于机器学习的形态学分析与基于物理模型的光谱拟合相结合，构建全自动框架。在EMIT数据上部署两种运行模式：(1) 每日摘要模式，自动处理所有下行数据并标记最大事件；(2) 回顾性分析模式，识别之前人工审查遗漏的羽流。

Abstract: Future imaging spectrometers will increase data volumes by orders of magnitude, requiring automated detection of trace gas point sources. We present a fully automated framework that combines machine learning-based morphological analysis with physics-based spectroscopic fitting to detect plumes without human participation. Applied to EMIT imaging spectrometer data, the system operates in two modes: "daily digest" that runs automatically on all downlinked data, flagging the largest events for immediate response, and a retrospective analysis that identifies plumes missed by prior human review. The daily digest demonstrates that a significant fraction of the largest plumes can be detected automatically with negligible false positives, while retrospective analysis suggests at least 25% of plumes may have been overlooked. In addition to the previously observed methane point sources, we extend detection to three understudied trace gases: NH3, NO2 and the first observations of carbon monoxide (CO) plume in EMIT imagery.

### [166] [Learning Dynamics of Zeroth-Order Optimization: A Kernel Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03373)
*Zhe Li,Bicheng Ying,Zidong Liu,Haibo Yang*

TL;DR: 本文通过引入经验神经正切核（eNTK）框架，解释了零阶（ZO）SGD方法在大语言模型（LLM）微调中成功的原因：ZO eNTK的近似误差取决于模型输出维度而非参数维度，从而具有维度无关性，为ZO方法在LLM中的可扩展性提供了理论依据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典优化理论认为ZO算法收敛速度随模型维度增加而下降，但近期实验表明ZO方法能成功应用于数百万亿参数的LLM微调。本文旨在解释这一理论与实践的矛盾。

Method: 推导了ZO SGD的单步学习动力学，揭示经验神经正切核（eNTK）是控制学习行为的关键项；通过分析发现ZO eNTK的每个元素对应于神经切向量投影到随机低维子空间的内积；利用Johnson-Lindenstrauss引理证明近似误差主要由扰动数量决定。

Result: ZO eNTK的近似误差依赖于模型输出大小而非庞大的参数维度，即具有维度无关性（dimension-free property），这为ZO方法在LLM微调中的可扩展性提供了理论支持。

Conclusion: 基于核的框架为理解ZO方法在学习动力学中的表现提供了新视角，解释了ZO方法在LLM微调中突破维度诅咒的根本原因。

Abstract: Classical optimization theory establishes that zeroth-order (ZO) algorithms suffer from a dimension-dependent slowdown, with convergence rates typically scaling with the model dimension compared to first-order methods. However, in contrast to these theoretical expectations, a growing body of recent work demonstrates the successful application of ZO methods to fine-tuning Large Language Models (LLMs) with billions of parameters. To explain this paradox, we derive the one-step learning dynamics of ZO SGD, where the empirical Neural Tangent Kernel (eNTK) naturally emerges as the key term governing the learning behavior. Inspection of the eNTK produced by ZO SGD reveals that each element corresponds to the inner product of neural tangent vectors projected onto a random low-dimensional subspace. Thus, by invoking the Johnson-Lindenstrauss Lemma, our analysis shows that the fidelity of the ZO eNTK is governed primarily by the number of perturbations. Crucially, the approximation error depends on the model output size rather than the massive parameter dimension. This dimension-free property provides a theoretical justification for the scalability of ZO methods to LLMs finetuning tasks. We believe that this kernel-based framework offers a novel perspective for understanding ZO methods within the context of learning dynamics.

In addition, we introduce a structured human evaluation protocol to assess the interpretability of generated rules along dimensions such as accuracy and usefulness. ### [168] [Two Calls, Two Moments, and the Vote-Accuracy Curve of Repeated LLM Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03379)
*Yi Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究LLM重复采样下多数投票的准确率边界。仅需一次和两次标记调用即可确定二项式正确性分布的均值和二阶矩，从而为任意固定预算的多数投票提供无需分布假设的精确边界（三原子极值解和二次对偶证书保证精确性）。三票边界有闭式解（宽度≤1/8）且含可认证改进准则；无限票极限边界尖锐但对阈值敏感。通过最大熵和LDGP点补全，实验（QNLI/QQP）验证三/五票准确率落在两调用投影区域内，温度变化和随机模型混合能产生不按一次调用准确率排序的投票增益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 重复采样是常用的测试时计算策略，但其收益受限于示例间正确性的潜在分布，而非单次调用的准确率。现有方法通常需要大量标记数据或分布假设来估计多数投票的收益，本文旨在通过最少标记信息（一次和两次调用）获得无需分布假设的精确边界。

Method: 将重复LLM推理视为条件独立同分布的二项式正确性层。使用一次标记调用估计平均成功概率（一阶矩），两次标记调用估计二阶矩，从而推导相同示例正确性相关性。通过将无限维矩问题简化为三原子极值解和二次对偶证书，获得任意固定多数投票预算的精确分布自由边界。三票边界有闭式解；无限票边界通过极限分析获得。辅以最大熵和Latent-difficulty Gaussian-probit (LDGP)点补全方法。

Result: 提出任意预算下的精确两调用置信区间。三票边界有闭式解且宽度≤1/8，含可认证改进准则。无限票边界尖锐但阈值敏感（依赖于q=1/2附近的潜在质量）。在QNLI和QQP数据集上，经验三/五票准确率落在投影区域内；温度变化和随机模型混合可产生不按单次调用准确率排序的投票增益。

Conclusion: 仅需两次标记调用即可精确界定多数投票的准确率边界，无需分布假设。该框架揭示了重复采样收益由潜在正确性分布而非单次准确率决定，为测试时计算分配提供了理论指导。温度变化和模型混合等策略能改变投票收益顺序，建议实践中关注二阶矩信息而非仅依赖单次调用准确率。

Abstract: Repeated sampling is a standard way to spend test-time compute, but its benefit is controlled by the latent distribution of correctness across examples, not by one-call accuracy alone. We study the binary correctness layer of repeated LLM inference under conditional-i.i.d. calls. One labeled call identifies the mean latent success probability; two labeled calls identify its second moment and hence the same-example correctness correlation that separates stable errors from recoverable call-level randomness. From these two moments, every fixed majority-vote budget has a sharp distribution-free two-call interval. The key technical reduction is that the infinite-dimensional moment problem has three-atom extremizers and quadratic dual certificates for every finite budget, so the bounds are exact rather than discretized or parametric. The first useful budget, three votes, has a closed form, width at most $1/8$, and a certified-improvement criterion. The infinite-vote endpoint is the limit of majority voting as the number of calls tends to infinity; it is also sharply bounded, but remains threshold-sensitive because it depends on latent mass around $q=1/2$. We add maximum-entropy and Latent-difficulty Gaussian-probit (LDGP) point completions, and experiments on LLM calls over QNLI and QQP show that empirical three- and five-vote accuracies are contained in the projected two-call regions while temperature changes and randomized model mixtures can create voting gains not ordered by one-call accuracy.

### [169] [Local Truncation Error-Guided Neural ODEs for Large Scale Traffic Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03386)
*Xiao Zhang,Yafei Li,Ruixiang Wang,Wei Wei,Shuo He,Mingliang Xu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出LTE-ODE，通过将局部截断误差（LTE）重新用作无监督前向归纳偏置，在不施加流形惩罚的情况下，在稳定区域保持高精度连续ODE演化，同时在异常点自适应触发离散补偿分支，解决了时空预测中连续宏观节律与离散微观冲击之间的连续性-冲击困境。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出LTE-ODE：将局部截断误差（LTE）映射为动态空间注意力掩码，在稳定区域保持高精度连续ODE演化，在冲击点自适应触发离散补偿分支；模型完全端到端训练，不使用流形惩罚。

Result: 在多个大规模基准数据集上取得最先进性能，展现出对高度非线性波动的卓越鲁棒性；积分步长消融实验表明模型具有高部署灵活性，能适应不同的硬件内存约束。

Conclusion: LTE-ODE通过将数值误差从"消除对象"重新定义为"无监督归纳偏置"，有效解决了连续-冲击两难问题，实现了高精度与鲁棒性的统一，且具备良好的实际部署灵活性。

Abstract: Spatiotemporal forecasting in physical systems, such as large-scale traffic networks, requires modeling a dual dynamic: continuous macroscopic rhythms and discrete, unpredictable microscopic shocks. While Neural Ordinary Differential Equations (ODEs) excel at capturing smooth evolution, their inherent Lipschitz continuity constraints inevitably cause severe over-smoothing when confronting abrupt anomalies. Recent physics-informed methods attempt to bypass this by penalizing numerical integration errors to enforce manifold smoothness. However, we mathematically reveal that such rigid regularization inherently triggers gradient conflicts and ``attention collapse,'' stripping the model of its sensitivity to anomalies. To resolve this continuity-shock dilemma, we propose Local Truncation Error-Guided Neural ODEs (LTE-ODE). Rather than treating numerical error as a nuisance to be eliminated, we innovatively repurpose the Local Truncation Error (LTE) as an unsupervised forward inductive bias. By mapping the LTE into a dynamic spatial attention mask, our architecture gracefully preserves high-precision continuous ODE evolution in stable regions, while adaptively triggering a discrete compensation branch exclusively at shock points. Trained purely end-to-end without manifold penalties, LTE-ODE achieves state-of-the-art performance on multiple large-scale benchmarks, exhibiting exceptional robustness against highly non-linear fluctuations. Furthermore, our ablation on integration steps demonstrates high deployment flexibility, allowing the model to seamlessly adapt to varying hardware memory constraints in real-world applications.

### [170] [Graph Reconstruction from Differentially Private GNN Explanations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03388)
*Rishi Raj Sahoo,Jyotirmaya Shivottam,Subhankar Mishra*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示差分隐私（DP）不足以保护GNN解释中的图结构隐私。提出的PRIVX攻击利用高斯DP机制与DDPM前向过程的等价性，通过反向扩散从DP扰动的解释中高精度重建隐藏图结构。实验表明在ε=5的常用隐私预算下，PRIVX在7个基准数据集的5个上AUC超过0.7。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有监管框架（如GDPR）要求ML预测附带事后解释，但释放解释存在隐私风险。虽然差分隐私被用作标准缓解手段，但其在GNN解释场景下的充分性尚未得到验证。本文旨在证明DP不足以保护图结构隐私，并量化不同因素对隐私泄露的影响。

Method: 1) 形式化PRIVX攻击：利用高斯DP机制等价于已知噪声水平σ(ε)的DDPM前向步骤，将图结构重建视为以DP扰动信号为条件的反向扩散过程（贝叶斯去噪器）。2) 构建分层敌手模型(M, \hatε, \hatδ, S, ρ)，在盲目攻击者和先知攻击者之间插值。3) 导出端点匹配的双边重建AUC界。4) 提出PRIVF诊断工具，共享相同扩散骨干，将泄露分解为解释器诱导成分和内在图分布成分。

Result: 在7个基准数据集、3种DP机制、3种GNN骨干网络上的实验表明：PRIVX在ε=5时在7个数据集的5个上AUC超过0.7，攻击在常用隐私预算下成功。对同质图，邻域聚合解释器（GraphLIME, GNNExplainer）比逐节点梯度解释器泄露更多结构；对强异质图，顺序反转。

Conclusion: 差分隐私不足以保护GNN解释中的图结构隐私，需要比单独DP更强的保护措施。PRIVF可有效诊断泄露来源，为实践者选择解释器提供分域指导。

Abstract: Regulatory frameworks such as GDPR increasingly require that ML predictions be accompanied by post-hoc explanations, even when raw data and trained models cannot be released. Differential privacy (DP) is the standard mitigation for the residual privacy risk of releasing these explanations. We show that DP is not sufficient: an adversary observing only DP-perturbed GNN explanations can reconstruct hidden graph structure with high accuracy. Our attack, PRIVX, exploits the fact that the Gaussian DP mechanism is a single DDPM forward step at known noise level σ(ε), recasting reconstruction as reverse diffusion conditioned on the corrupted signal, a principled Bayesian denoiser under known DP corruption. We formalise a stratified adversary model parameterised by (M, \hatε, \hatδ, S, ρ) that interpolates between oblivious and oracle attackers, and derive endpoint-matched two-sided bounds on reconstruction AUC. For practitioners, we provide regime-stratified guidance on explainer choice: on homophilic graphs, neighbourhood-aggregating explainers (GraphLIME, GNNExplainer) leak more structure than per-node gradient explainers under the same DP budget; on strongly heterophilic graphs the ordering reverses. We introduce PRIVF as an auxiliary diagnostic sharing the same diffusion backbone to decompose leakage into explainer-induced and intrinsic graph-distribution components. Experiments across seven benchmarks, three DP mechanisms, and three GNN backbones show PRIVX achieves AUC above 0.7 at ε = 5 on five of seven datasets, with the attack succeeding well within typically deployed privacy budgets.

*Onkar Jadhav,Tim French,Matthew Rayson,Nicole L. Jones*

Abstract: Probabilistic super-resolution of high-dimensional spatial fields using diffusion models is often computationally prohibitive due to the cost of operating directly in pixel space. We propose PODiff, a structured conditional generative framework that performs diffusion in a fixed, variance-ordered Proper Orthogonal Decomposition (POD) coefficient space, exploiting the orthogonality of POD modes to impose an interpretable, variance-ordered latent geometry. This design enables efficient ensemble generation, preserves dominant spatial structure, and yields spatially interpretable, well-calibrated uncertainty at substantially lower computational cost. We evaluate PODiff on sea surface temperature downscaling over the West Australian coast and on a controlled advection-diffusion benchmark. PODiff achieves reconstruction accuracy comparable to pixel-space diffusion while requiring significantly less memory and producing more reliable uncertainty estimates than deterministic and Monte Carlo Dropout baselines.

Conclusion: 推断显式解释性理论比纯预测更接近人类认知发展中的理解本质，NEO通过组合式程序学习为世界建模提供了新的范式。

Abstract: What does it mean to understand the world? Contemporary world models often operationalize understanding as accurate future prediction in latent or observation space. Developmental cognitive science, however, suggests a different view: human understanding emerges through the construction of internal theories of how the world works, even before mature language is acquired. Inspired by this theory-building view of cognition, we introduce Learning-to-Theorize, a learning paradigm for inferring explicit explanatory theories of the world from raw, non-textual observations. We instantiate this paradigm with the Neural Theorizer (NEO), a probabilistic neural model that induces latent programs as a learned Language of Thought and executes them through a shared transition model. In NEO, a theory is represented as an executable, compositional program whose learned primitives can be systematically recombined to explain novel phenomena. ### [174] [FIBER: A Differentially Private Optimizer with Filter-Aware Innovation Bias Correction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03425)
*Duc Dm,Thao Do,Minh Son Hoang,Anh Le Duc Tran,Daeyoung Kim,Huy Nguyen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: FiBeR是一种专为时间滤波私有化梯度设计的差分隐私优化器，通过创新空间中的去噪、解耦观测几何与创新增益、以及滤波感知的二阶矩校准，在多个视觉和语言基准上超越了现有最先进方法。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的差分隐私训练方法在自适应优化器（如AdamW）中使用时间滤波减少梯度噪声方差时，滤波操作改变了DP噪声统计特性，导致原有的偏置校正（如减去sigma_w^2）失效，需要重新设计适配滤波场景的DP优化器。

Method: FiBeR包含三种关键技术：(i) 在创新空间中进行去噪——对残差流滤波后积分形成滤波梯度估计；(ii) 解耦两点观测几何与创新增益，实现独立调参；(iii) 引入滤波感知的二阶矩校准，减去衰减后的DP噪声贡献A(ω)σ_w^2，其中A(ω)对创新滤波器有闭式解，对一般稳定线性滤波器可计算。

Result: 在视觉和语言基准任务上，FiBeR在相同隐私预算下持续显著提升DP优化器性能，在多项任务中超越当前最优结果。

Conclusion: FiBeR通过专门设计适配时间滤波梯度场景的机制，有效解决了滤波与DP噪声统计之间的交互问题，为差分隐私训练提供了更优的优化器方案。

Abstract: Differentially private (DP) training protects individual examples by adding noise to gradients, but the injected noise interacts nontrivially with adaptive optimizers. Recent DP methods temporally filter privatized gradients to reduce variance; however, filtering also changes the DP noise statistics seen by AdamW's second-moment accumulator. As a result, bias corrections derived for unfiltered DP noise, such as subtracting sigma_w squared, can become miscalibrated when filtering is present.
  We propose FiBeR, a DP optimizer designed for temporally filtered privatized gradients. FiBeR (i) performs denoising in innovation space by filtering the residual stream and integrating it to form the filtered gradient estimate, (ii) decouples the two-point observation geometry from the innovation gain to enable independent tuning, and (iii) introduces a filter-aware second-moment calibration that subtracts the attenuated DP noise contribution A(omega) sigma_w squared, where A(omega) is derived in closed form for the innovation filter and can be computed for general stable linear filters.
  Across vision and language benchmarks, FiBeR consistently demonstrates substantial improvements in the performance of DP optimizers, surpassing state-of-the-art results under equivalent privacy constraints on multiple tasks.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Solving inverse problems in dynamical systems governed by high-dimensional coupled ordinary differential equations (ODEs) is a ubiquitous challenge in scientific machine learning. In many real-world applications, researchers seek to uncover unknown parameters or model unknown dynamics even as the underlying physics is only partially characterized, and observations are sparse and limited to specific measurable channels. While physics-informed neural networks (PINNs) are ideal for inverse inference under partial observability, existing PINNs typically rely on task-specific joint optimization, which suffers from optimization difficulties and poor generalization. In this paper, we propose a meta-inverse physics-informed neural network (MI-PINN) that reformulates inverse modeling as a two-stage meta-learning problem. MI-PINN first learns a physics-aware representation across multiple tasks, and then performs inverse modeling by optimizing task-specific unknowns while keeping the learned representation fixed. This two-stage formulation significantly reduces the parameter search dimension, thereby improving sample efficiency and enabling accurate inference. To handle multi-scale dynamics common in these high-dimensional ODE systems, we further introduce an adaptive clustering-based multi-branch learning scheme. We demonstrate the effectiveness of MI-PINN on whole-body physiologically based pharmacokinetic (PBPK) models with up to 33 coupled ODEs, using paracetamol and theophylline under intravenous and oral dosing scenarios. Experimental results show that MI-PINN enables accurate recovery of masked kinetic parameters and reconstruction of missing mechanistic terms despite limited clinical observations.

### [180] [PerFlow: Physics-Embedded Rectified Flow for Efficient Reconstruction and Uncertainty Quantification of Spatiotemporal Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03548)
*Hao Zhou,Rui Zhang,Han Wan,Hao Sun*

<details>

Method: PerFlow 将观测条件化与物理约束解耦：1) 通过无引导条件化将观测数据直接馈入整流流动力学；2) 通过约束保持投影（如不可压缩性或守恒律）嵌入硬物理约束。理论证明该设计保证了采样轨迹的物理一致流形不变性。

Generative models, by learning distributions over spatiotemporal fields, can better handle sparsity and uncertainty. However, existing generative approaches enforce data consistency and PDE constraints simultaneously via sampling-time gradient guidance, resulting in slow and unstable inference. To this end, we propose PerFlow, a Physics-embedded rectified Flow for efficient sparse reconstruction and uncertainty quantification of spatiotemporal dynamics. PerFlow decouples observation conditioning from physics enforcement, performing guidance-free conditioning by feeding observations into rectified-flow dynamics while embedding hard physics via a constraint-preserving projection (e.g., incompressibility or conservation). ### [181] [HeadQ: Model-Visible Distortion and Score-Space Correction for KV-Cache Quantization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03562)
*Jorge L. Ruiz Williams*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出KV缓存量化应在模型可见坐标（而非存储空间）中衡量误差。对于键（Key），提出HeadQ方法，通过低秩残差侧码在查询基中进行加性logit校正；对于值（Value），使用A²加权令牌失真代理。实验表明，Fisher/分数空间误差比原始键MSE能更好预测注意力KL散度，HeadQ在2-bit量化下可消除84-94%的额外困惑度。

Method: 1) 键侧：提出HeadQ，学习一个低秩残差侧码，在校准阶段学习的查询基中表示，并作为加性logit校正应用；2) 值侧：使用固定注意力下的A²加权令牌失真代理；3) 通过Fisher/分数空间误差而非原始MSE来预测注意力KL散度。

Conclusion: KV缓存量化应以模型可见坐标（logit空间和注意力加权读出空间）中的误差为优化目标，HeadQ方法和A²加权值策略能有效改进量化性能，消除大部分因量化引入的困惑度损失。

Abstract: KV-cache quantizers usually optimize storage-space reconstruction, even though attention reads keys through logits and values through attention-weighted readout. We argue that persistent cache error should be measured in model-visible coordinates. For keys, the visible object is score error modulo constant shifts; this yields HeadQ, a key-side method that stores a low-rank residual side code in a calibration-learned query basis and applies it as an additive logit correction. For values, fixed-attention readout gives an $A^2$-weighted token-distortion surrogate. Across six models, Fisher/score-space error predicts attention KL far better than raw key MSE; same-budget counterexamples, null-space interventions, query-PCA controls, and wrong-sign HeadQ falsify storage-MSE alternatives. In K-only WikiText-103 decode experiments with dense values, HeadQ removes roughly $84$--$94\%$ of the excess perplexity on the strongest 2-bit rows; in an auxiliary full-KV 2-bit composition, HeadQ plus an $A^2$ value policy improves all six models.

*He Lyu,Huolin Zeng,Junren Wang,Huazhen Yang,Linchao He,Yong Chen,Zhirui Li,Andreas Maier,Siming Bayer,Huan Song*

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于统一Transformer的多任务学习框架，通过正交任务分解（OrthTD）将患者表示拆分为共享子空间和任务特定子空间，并施加几何正交约束来减少冗余、隔离任务特定信号。在12,430名手术患者的真实队列中，预测四个结局的AUC达87.5%，AUPRC达37.2%，优于现有方法，特别是在不平衡数据中识别罕见事件方面表现突出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有硬参数共享方法在任务梯度冲突时会导致负迁移，而灵活共享方法仍可能纠缠共享信号与任务特定信号，缺乏有效平衡共享表示学习与任务特定建模的手段。

Method: 基于统一Transformer进行多模态融合，加入正交任务分解（OrthTD），将患者表示分解为共享子空间和任务特定子空间，并通过几何正交性约束减少冗余、隔离任务特定信号。

Result: 在12,430名手术患者队列上预测四个结局，平均AUC 87.5%，平均AUPRC 37.2%，一致优于先进的表格数据方法和多任务方法，特别是在AUPRC上取得显著提升。

Conclusion: 强制共享表示与任务特定表示非冗余可以改善多模态临床数据上的多结局预测性能。

Abstract: Real-world clinical data is inherently multimodal, providing complementary evidence that mirrors the practical necessity of jointly assessing multiple related outcomes. Although multi-task learning can improve efficiency by sharing information across outcomes, existing approaches often fail to balance shared representation learning with outcome-specific modeling. Hard parameter sharing can trigger negative transfer when task gradients conflict, while flexible sharing may still entangle shared and task-specific signals. To address this, we propose a multi-task framework built on a unified Transformer for multimodal fusion, augmented with Orthogonal Task Decomposition (OrthTD) to split patient representations into shared and task-specific subspaces and impose a geometric orthogonality constraint to reduce redundancy and isolate task-specific signals. We evaluated OrthTD on a real-world cohort of 12,430 surgical patients for predicting four outcomes. OrthTD achieved average AUC (area under the receiver operating characteristic curve) of 87.5% and average AUPRC (area under the precision-recall curve) of 37.2%, consistently outperformed advanced tabular and multi-task methods. Notably, OrthTD achieves substantial gains in AUPRC, indicating superior performance in identifying rare events within imbalanced clinical data. These results suggest that enforcing non-redundant shared and task-specific representations can improve multi-outcome prediction from multimodal clinical data.

### [184] [Flow Matching on Symmetric Spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03588)
*Francesco Ruscelli,Ferdinando Zanchetta,Rita Fioresi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种在黎曼对称空间（包括球面、双曲空间和Grassmannian流形）上训练流匹配模型的通用框架，通过利用对称空间的代数结构，将流匹配问题转化为其等距群李代数子空间上的流匹配，从而线性化问题并简化测地线处理。在实Grassmannian流形上展示了该框架的应用。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用黎曼对称空间的代数结构，将对称空间上的流匹配重新表述为等距群李代数子空间上的流匹配，从而将问题线性化，简化了测地线的处理。

Result: 在实Grassmannian流形SO(n)/SO(k)×SO(n-k)上成功展示了该框架的应用。

Abstract: We introduce a general framework for training flow matching models on Riemannian symmetric spaces, a large class of manifolds that includes the sphere, hyperbolic space and Grassmannians. We exploit their algebraic structure to reformulate flow matching on symmetric spaces as flow matching on a subspace of the Lie algebra of their isometry group, thus linearizing the problem and greatly simplifying the handling of geodesics. As an application, we showcase our framework on the real Grassmannians $\operatorname{SO}(n) / \operatorname{SO}(k) \times \operatorname{SO}(n-k)$.

### [185] [ELAS: Efficient Pre-Training of Low-Rank Large Language Models via 2:4 Activation Sparsity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03667)
*Jiaxi Li,Lu Yin,Li Shen,Jinjin Xu,Yuhui Liu,Wenwu Wang,Shiwei Liu,Xilu Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出ELAS框架，通过在低秩LLM的前馈网络中应用平方ReLU激活函数并实现2:4结构化激活稀疏性，在保持模型性能的同时显著降低训练内存开销并加速训练与推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有低秩训练方法通常保留全秩激活矩阵，主导了内存消耗并限制了大批量训练的吞吐量；而直接对权重应用稀疏性会导致不可忽视的性能下降。亟需一种既能利用2:4结构化稀疏性优势又不牺牲性能的高效预训练方法。

Method: ELAS框架：在低秩模型的FFN层中使用平方ReLU激活函数，并在平方ReLU操作之后对激活值施加2:4结构化稀疏性，从而利用NVIDIA GPU对2:4稀疏格式的原生支持。

Result: 在60M到1B参数的LLaMA模型上的预训练实验表明，ELAS在应用2:4激活稀疏性后性能下降极小，同时实现了训练和推理加速，并显著降低了激活内存开销，尤其在大批量场景下效果更明显。

Conclusion: ELAS成功地将2:4结构化激活稀疏性与低秩训练相结合，为大规模LLM的高效预训练提供了一种可行的方案，能够在保持性能的同时大幅提升资源效率。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have achieved remarkable capabilities, but their immense computational demands during training remain a critical bottleneck for widespread adoption. Low-rank training has received attention in recent years due to its ability to significantly reduce training memory usage. Meanwhile, applying 2:4 structured sparsity to weights and activations to leverage NVIDIA GPU support for 2:4 structured sparse format has become a promising direction. However, existing low-rank methods often leave activation matrices in full-rank, which dominates memory consumption and limits throughput during large-batch training. Furthermore, directly applying sparsity to weights often leads to non-negligible performance degradation. To achieve efficient pre-training of LLMs, this paper proposes ELAS: Efficient pre-training of Low-rank LLMs via 2:4 Activation Sparsity, a novel framework for low-rank models via 2:4 activation sparsity. ELAS applies squared ReLU activation functions to the feed-forward networks in low-rank models and implements 2:4 structured sparsity on the activations after the squared ReLU operation. We evaluated ELAS through pre-training experiments on LLaMA models ranging from 60M to 1B parameters. The results demonstrate that ELAS maintains performance with minimal degradation after applying 2:4 activation sparsity, while achieving training and inference acceleration. Moreover, ELAS reduces activation memory overhead, particularly with large batch sizes. Code is available at ELAS Repo.

</details>

### [187] [Most ReLU Networks Admit Identifiable Parameters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03601)
*Moritz Grillo,Guido Montúfar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究深度ReLU网络的实现映射，引入基于加权多面体复形的框架分析参数冗余，证明对于输入和隐含层宽度至少为2的架构，存在可辨识参数的开集，表明功能维度等于参数数减去隐含神经元数，并建立了深度层次结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解深度ReLU网络中参数与函数之间的对应关系，揭示除缩放和排列对称性之外隐藏的冗余性，确定何时函数能唯一确定其参数。

Method: 引入基于加权多面体复形的分析框架，通过研究深度ReLU网络的实现映射，分析参数的可辨识性和功能维度。

Result: 对于输入和隐含层宽度至少为2的架构，存在可辨识参数的开集；功能维度等于参数数减去隐含神经元数；最小功能表示仍存在非平凡参数冗余；建立了泛深度层次结构。

Conclusion: 深度ReLU网络存在广泛的可辨识性，且深度具有本质优势——更深的网络无法被更浅的网络泛化表示。

Abstract: We study the realization map of deep ReLU networks, focusing on when a function determines its parameters up to scaling and permutation. To analyze hidden redundancies beyond these standard symmetries, we introduce a framework based on weighted polyhedral complexes. Our main result shows that for every architecture whose input and hidden layers have width at least two, there exists an open set of identifiable parameters. This implies that the functional dimension of every such architecture is exactly the number of parameters minus the number of hidden neurons. We further show that minimal functional representations can still have non-trivial parameter redundancies. Finally, we establish a generic depth hierarchy, whereby for an open set of parameters the realized function cannot be represented generically by any shallower network.

### [188] [Rethinking the Rank Threshold for LoRA Fine-Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03724)
*Juneyoung Park*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对LoRA微调在神经正切核（NTK）机制下的秩需求问题，给出了三个理论结果，将二分类场景下的推荐秩从r≥12降低到r=1：1）使用非对称LoRA流形维度替代Sard计数得到更弱的容量条件；2）交叉熵损失下Polyak-Łojasiewicz不等式消除了秩阈值；3）Rademacher复杂度界预测当偏置项饱和时秩一方差最优。实验验证了二分类任务中秩一的竞争力，而多分类任务的最优秩高于一，符合理论预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有工作证明在平方误差损失下，LoRA微调避免伪局部极小值的充分条件是秩满足r(r+1)/2 > KN，这导致在标准少样本RoBERTa设置中要求r≥12。然而这一条件对于特定场景（如二分类）是否必要，以及其在使用交叉熵损失（实际微调中使用的损失函数）时的适用性尚不清楚。

Method: 1) 理论推导：用非对称LoRA流形维度替代对称Sard计数，推导更弱的容量条件；在交叉熵损失下利用PL不等式分析秩阈值；通过Rademacher复杂度界分析秩一方差最优性条件。2) 实验验证：在四个GLUE风格的二分类任务、三种编码器架构以及RoBERTa-large规模上进行对比实验。

Result: 理论结果表明在二分类场景下秩一即可满足条件；实验证明在二分类任务中秩一与秩十二竞争力相当，而在多分类MNLI任务中最优秩高于一。

Conclusion: 在NTK框架的二分类场景下，LoRA秩可降至一；多分类场景的最优秩更高，留给未来工作。

Abstract: A recent landscape analysis of LoRA fine-tuning in the neural tangent kernel regime establishes a sufficient condition $r(r+1)/2 > KN$ on the LoRA rank $r$ for the absence of spurious local minima under squared-error loss, prescribing $r \geq 12$ on canonical few-shot RoBERTa setups. The condition is stated for general output dimension $K$, so its sharpness in any particular regime, and its practical implication for the cross-entropy loss actually used in fine-tuning, are open. We give three results that together reduce the prescribed rank to $r = 1$ for binary classification in this regime. First, replacing the symmetric Sard-form count with the non-symmetric LoRA manifold dimension yields a strictly weaker capacity requirement, $r(m+n) - r^2 > C^* \cdot KN$ with $C^* \approx 1.35$ under Gaussian-iid features, satisfied at $r = 1$ on canonical setups. Second, in the cross-entropy setting the Polyak--Łojasiewicz inequality removes the rank threshold entirely. Third, a Rademacher-complexity bound predicts rank-one variance optimality precisely when the bias term is saturated, which is the case for binary classification but not for $K > 2$. Empirically, across four GLUE-style binary tasks, three encoder architectures, and at scale on RoBERTa-large, rank one is competitive with the existing prescription $r = 12$; on multi-class MNLI the optimal rank shifts above one, also as predicted. The binary-regime guarantees are conditional on standard NTK assumptions; the multi-class extension is left to future work.

</details>

*Zhiqi Li,Duowen Chen,Yuchen Sun,Bo Zhu*

Motivation: 受物理传输中流映射技术启发，旨在统一现有扩散模型和流模型，实现高效少步生成，避免对特定预测实例化的依赖。

Method: 提出累积流抽象，引入累积参数化，仅需对时间嵌入和训练目标做最小修改，无需增加模型容量，即可将现有扩散/流模型转化为少步生成框架。

Result: 在图像生成、几何分布建模、联合预测和SDF生成等任务上验证有效性，在保持合成质量的同时显著降低推理成本。

Abstract: We propose a unified, few-step generative modeling framework based on \emph{cumulative flow maps} for long-range transport in probability space, inspired by flow-map techniques for physical transport and dynamics. At its core is a cumulative-flow abstraction that connects local, instantaneous updates with finite-time transport, enabling generative models to reason about global state transitions. This perspective yields a unified few-step framework built on cumulative transport and \revise{cumulative} parameterization that applies broadly to existing diffusion- and flow-based models without being tied to a specific prediction \revise{instantiation}. Our formulation supports few-step and even one-step generation while preserving synthesis quality, requiring only minimal changes to time embeddings and training objectives, and no increase in model capacity. We demonstrate its effectiveness across diverse tasks, including image generation, geometric distribution modeling, joint prediction, and SDF generation, with reduced inference cost.

### [190] [Spatiotemporal Convolutions on EEG signal -- A Representation Learning Perspective on Efficient and Explainable EEG Classification with Convolutional Neural Nets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03874)
*Laurits Dixen,Stefan Heinrich,Paolo Burelli*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究在BCI运动想象分类任务中，将传统的独立一维（1D）空间和时间卷积替换为二维（2D）时空卷积。实验表明，2D卷积在高维任务中能显著减少训练时间且保持性能不变，尽管1D和2D模型在表示几何上存在显著差异，但在频谱特征重要性上无差异。最终提出使用2D卷积层的改进模型，并强调从内部表示角度理解架构编码的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有浅层CNN通常沿空间和时间维度使用独立的1D卷积层，且两者之间缺乏非线性激活层直接拼接。作者希望探究一种替代方案——使用2D时空卷积，考察其对学习过程的影响以及性能与效率的权衡。

Method: 对比三种模型：1D CNN、2D CNN以及CNN+Transformer混合模型；在低维（3通道）和高维（22通道）BCI运动想象分类任务上进行实验；通过训练时间、分类性能、频谱特征重要性分析及表示相似性分析（Representational Similarity Analysis）进行多维度评估。

Result: 2D卷积在高维任务中显著缩短训练时间，同时保持与1D卷积相当的分类性能；在频谱特征重要性上两者无差异；但1D与2D模型在内部表示的几何结构上存在显著差异。

Conclusion: 推荐采用2D卷积层构建模型以实现更快的训练和推理；指出架构驱动的编码方式对处理复杂多变量信号具有重要影响，这种影响更体现在内部表示层面而非仅靠性能指标衡量。

Abstract: Classification of EEG signals using shallow Convolutional Neural Networks (CNNs) is a prevalent and successful approach across a variety of fields. Most of these models use independent one-dimensional (1D) convolutional layers along the spatial and temporal dimensions, which are concatenated without a non-linear activation layer between. In this paper, we investigate an alternative encoding that operates a bi-dimensional (2D) spatiotemporal convolution. While 2D convolutions are numerically identical to two concatenated 1D convolutions along the two dimensions, the impact on learning is still uncertain. We test 1D and 2D CNNs and a CNN+transformer hybrid model in a low-dimensional (3-channel) and a high-dimensional (22-channel) BCI motor imagery classification task. We observe that 2D convolutions significantly reduce training time in high-dimensional tasks while maintaining performance. We investigate the root of this improvement and find no difference in spectral feature importance. However, a clear pattern emerges in representational similarity across models: 1D and 2D models yield vastly different representational geometries. Overall, we suggest an improved model with a 2D convolutional layer for faster training and inference. We also highlight the importance of architecturally-driven encoding when processing complex multivariate signals, as reflected in internal representations rather than purely in performance metrics.

</details>


### [191] [Information Plane Analysis of Binary Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03636)
*Maximilian Nothnagel,Bernhard C. Geiger*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过二值神经网络（BNN）对信息平面分析进行统计验证，发现传统MI估计在高维确定性表示中容易饱和到log₂N，导致分析失效。在可靠估计条件下，训练375个BNN后发现：晚期压缩阶段虽常见，但压缩表示与泛化性能之间并无一致相关性，二者关系高度依赖于任务、架构和正则化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 信息平面分析（IP分析）通过互信息（MI）研究深度神经网络训练动态，但由于从高维确定性表示中估计MI存在统计困难，其统计有效性常受到质疑。本文旨在系统研究这种统计失效问题，并揭示压缩与泛化之间真实关系。

Method: 在二值神经网络（BNN）上进行IP分析（因激活离散、MI有限）；使用插件熵估计器表征有限样本行为，识别样本量N和表示维度D的可靠估计区间；在可靠区间内训练375个BNN，系统考察晚期压缩阶段的存在性及压缩表示与泛化性能的关系。

Result: 识别出MI估计可靠与不可靠的参数区间；不可靠区间内经验MI估计饱和到log₂N，使IP轨迹失去信息量；可靠区间内观察到晚期压缩频繁出现，但压缩表示与泛化性能无一致相关性。

Conclusion: 压缩与泛化之间的关系高度依赖任务、架构和正则化，并非简单相关。研究强调了进行IP分析时统计可靠性检查的必要性。

Abstract: Information plane (IP) analysis has been suggested to study the training dynamics of deep neural networks through mutual information (MI) between inputs, representations, and targets. However, its statistical validity is often compromised by the difficulty of estimating MI from samples of high-dimensional, deterministic representations.
  In this work, we perform IP analyses on binary neural networks (BNNs) where activations are discrete and MI is finite. We characterise the finite-sample behaviour of the plug-in entropy estimator and identify regimes for sample size $N$ and representation dimensionality $D$ under which MI estimates are reliable. Outside these regimes, we show that empirical MI estimates saturate to $\log_2 N$, rendering IP trajectories uninformative.
  Restricting attention to the reliable regime, we train 375 BNNs to investigate the existence of late-stage compression phases and the relationship between compressed representations and generalisation performance. Our results show that while late-stage compression is frequently observed, compressed latent representations do not consistently correlate with improved generalization performance. Instead, the relationship between compression and generalisation is highly dependent on task, architecture, and regularisation.

### [192] [Flow Sampling: Learning to Sample from Unnormalized Densities via Denoising Conditional Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03984)
*Aaron Havens,Brian Karrer,Neta Shaul*

TL;DR: Flow Sampling 是一种基于扩散模型和流匹配的无数据采样框架，通过从能量函数构造的去噪扩散漂移进行回归训练，高效地从未归一化密度中采样，并支持欧氏空间和黎曼流形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从未归一化密度中采样时，评估能量函数的成本往往很高，因此核心挑战是学习一个高效的采样器。现有方法在计算效率和可扩展性方面存在不足，且难以扩展到非欧氏空间。

Method: 提出 Flow Sampling 框架，基于扩散模型和流匹配，在无数据设置下训练。目标函数以噪声样本为条件，回归到从能量函数构造的去噪扩散漂移（与标准扩散模型以数据样本为条件回归到加噪扩散漂移相反）。利用插值过程最小化训练期间的能量函数评估次数，并推导了常曲率流形（包括超球面和双曲空间）上条件漂移的闭式公式。

Result: 在合成能量基准、小肽、大规模摊销分子构象生成以及球面分布等多个任务上取得了强经验性能，证明了方法的高效性和可扩展性。

Conclusion: Flow Sampling 提供了一种高效、可扩展且适用于多种几何结构的未归一化密度采样方法，在计算效率和性能上具有优势。

Abstract: Sampling from unnormalized densities is analogous to the generative modeling problem, but the target distribution is defined by a known energy function instead of data samples. Because evaluating the energy function is often costly, a primary challenge is to learn an efficient sampler. We introduce Flow Sampling, a framework built on diffusion models and flow matching for the data-free setting. Our training objective is conditioned on a noise sample and regresses onto a denoising diffusion drift constructed from the energy function. In contrast, diffusion models' objective is conditioned on a data sample and regresses onto a noising diffusion drift. We utilize the interpolant process to minimize the number of energy function evaluations during training, resulting in an efficient and scalable method for sampling unnormalized densities. Furthermore, our formulation naturally extends to Riemannian manifolds, enabling diffusion-based sampling in geometries beyond Euclidean space. We derive a closed-form formula for the conditional drift on constant curvature manifolds, including hyperspheres and hyperbolic spaces. We evaluate Flow Sampling on synthetic energy benchmarks, small peptides, large-scale amortized molecular conformer generation, and distributions supported on the sphere, demonstrating strong empirical performance.

Building on this insight, we propose Uni-OPD, a unified OPD framework that generalizes across Large Language Models (LLMs) and Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs), centered on a dual-perspective optimization strategy. Specifically, from the student's perspective, we adopt two data balancing strategies to promote exploration of informative student-generated states during training. From the teacher's perspective, we show that reliable supervision hinges on whether aggregated token-level guidance remains order-consistent with the outcome reward. To this end, we develop an outcome-guided margin calibration mechanism to restore order consistency between correct and incorrect trajectories. Abstract: Matrix-based optimizers have demonstrated immense potential in training Large Language Models (LLMs), however, designing an ideal optimizer remains a formidable challenge. A superior optimizer must satisfy three core desiderata: efficiency, achieving Muon-like preconditioning to accelerate optimization; stability, strictly adhering to the scale-invariance inherent in neural networks; and speed, minimizing computational overhead. While existing methods address these aspects to varying degrees, they often fail to unify them, either incurring prohibitive computational costs like Muon, or allowing radial jitters that compromise stability like RMNP. To bridge this gap, we propose Nora, an optimizer that rigorously satisfies all three requirements. Nora achieves training stability by explicitly stabilizing weight norms and angular velocities through row-wise momentum projection onto the orthogonal complement of the weights. Simultaneously, by leveraging the block-diagonal dominance of the Transformer Hessian, Nora effectively approximates structured preconditioning while maintaining an optimal computational complexity of $\mathcal{O}(mn)$. ### [198] [Realizable Bayes-Consistency for General Metric Losses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03823)
*Dan Tsir Cohen,Steve Hanneke,Aryeh Kontorovich*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了在可实现设定下，使用一般度量损失进行学习时的强通用贝叶斯一致性，将经典刻画从0-1分类和实值回归扩展到了更一般的度量损失场景。主要贡献是：给出了假设类H存在分布无关学习规则（其风险几乎必然收敛到零）的充要条件，该条件基于一种新的组合障碍——无限非递减(γ_k)-Littlestone树（其中γ_k→∞）。

Method: 引入无限非递减(γ_k)-Littlestone树的概念（其中γ_k→∞），将Bousquet等人（2021）和Hanneke（2021）在0-1分类中使用的Littlestone树结构以及Attias等人（2024）在实值回归中的方法扩展到一般的度量损失设定中，从而给出可实现情形下的充要条件刻画。

Given an instance space $(\mathcal X,ρ)$, a label space $(\mathcal Y,\ell)$ with possibly unbounded loss, and a hypothesis class $\mathcal H \subseteq \mathcal Y^{\mathcal X}$, we resolve the realizable case of an open problem presented in \citet{pmlr-v178-cohen22a}. Specifically, we find the necessary and sufficient conditions on the hypothesis class $\mathcal H$ under which there exists a distribution-free learning rule whose risk converges almost surely to the best-in-class risk (which is zero) for every realizable data-generating distribution. Our main contribution is this sharp characterization in terms of a combinatorial obstruction: Similarly to \citet{attias2024optimallearnersrealizableregression}, we introduce the notion of an infinite non-decreasing $(γ_k)$-Littlestone tree, where $γ_k \to \infty$. This extends the Littlestone tree structure used in \citet{bousquet_theory_2021} to the metric loss setting.

Motivation: 大型医院训练的机器学习模型难以直接迁移到小型医院，因为不同地区医疗数据的测量分布和频率存在显著差异，模型泛化能力不足。

Method: 构建跨区域迁移基准，将模型从源域迁移到不同地区视为域增量学习问题，评估数据回放和弹性权重巩固（EWC）两种方法。

Result: 发现美国不同地区医疗数据的测量分布和频率存在显著差异，验证了所提基准的有效性。

Conclusion: 域增量学习方法是解决跨医院模型迁移泛化问题的有效途径，但需要进一步研究以提升迁移效果。

Abstract: In recent years, machine learning has made significant progress in clinical outcome prediction, demonstrating increasingly accurate results. However, the substantial resources required for hospitals to train these models, such as data collection, labeling, and computational power, limit the feasibility for smaller hospitals to develop their own models. An alternative approach involves transferring a machine learning model trained by a large hospital to smaller hospitals, allowing them to fine-tune the model on their specific patient data.
  However, these models are often trained and validated on data from a single hospital, raising concerns about their generalizability to new data. Our research shows that there are notable differences in measurement distributions and frequencies across various regions in the United States. To address this, we propose a benchmark that tests a machine learning model's ability to transfer from a source domain to different regions across the country. This benchmark assesses a model's capacity to learn meaningful information about each new domain while retaining key features from the original domain.
  Using this benchmark, we frame the transfer of a machine learning model from one region to another as a domain incremental learning problem. While the task of patient outcome prediction remains the same, the input data distribution varies, necessitating a model that can effectively manage these shifts. We evaluate two popular domain incremental learning methods: data replay, which stores examples from previous data sources for fine-tuning on the current source, and Elastic Weight Consolidation (EWC), a model parameter regularization method that maintains features important for both data sources.

### [200] [Complex Equation Learner: Rational Symbolic Regression with Gradient Descent in Complex Domain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03841)
*Sergei Garmaev,Maurice Gauché,Olga Fink*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出复数权重扩展的Equation Learner方法，通过允许优化轨迹绕过实轴退化路径，解决了含奇点算子（除法、对数、平方根）的符号回归问题，在基准测试和实验数据上验证了有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于梯度的符号回归方法（如Equation Learner）在处理包含除法、对数、平方根等引入奇点或定义域约束的算子时存在优化困难，通常只能避免使用这些算子或施加限制（如约束分母避免极点），导致假设空间受限，无法发现包含奇点行为的真实物理方程。

Method: 提出Equation Learner的复数权重扩展，将网络权重扩展至复数域，使得优化轨迹能够绕过实轴上的退化路径（如分母为零、负数取对数等），从而在目标表达式具有实域极点时也能稳定收敛，实现对除法、对数、平方根等算子的无约束使用。

Result: 在符号回归基准测试上验证了方法的有效性，并表明该方法能够从实验频响数据中恢复包含奇点行为的目标表达式。

Conclusion: 复数权重扩展有效缓解了实值优化中的退化和奇点问题，使得Equation Learner能够以无约束方式处理更广泛的算子，扩展了可发现的符号表达式类别，尤其适用于包含极点、对数分支等奇异行为的物理系统建模。

Abstract: Symbolic regression aims to discover interpretable equations from data, yet modern gradient-based methods fail for operators that introduce singularities or domain constraints, including division, logarithms, and square roots. As a result, Equation Learner-type models typically avoid these operators or impose restrictions, e.g. constraining denominators to prevent poles, which narrows the hypothesis class. We propose a complex weight extension of the Equation Learner that mitigates real-valued optimization pathologies by allowing optimization trajectories to bypass real-axis degeneracies. The proposed approach converges stably even when the target expression has real-domain poles, and it enables unconstrained use of operations such as logarithm and square root. We Validate the method on symbolic regression benchmarks and show it can recover singular behavior from experimental frequency response data.

*Ryan King,Gang Li,Bobak Mortazavi,Tianbao Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出一种面向CLIP模型的内存高效、分布鲁棒的增量学习方法，通过动态重加权各类别损失来缓解灾难性遗忘，在少量内存下即可有效适应新数据。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出一种分布鲁棒的方法，在训练过程中根据每个类别的损失动态重加权，实现内存高效的增量学习。

Result: 在类增量设置（CIFAR-100、ImageNet1K）和域增量设置（DomainNet）上，该方法即使在使用极少量内存的情况下也能快速适应CLIP模型并最小化灾难性遗忘。

Abstract: Contrastive Language-Image Pretraining (CLIP) models excel at understanding image-text relationships but struggle with adapting to new data without forgetting prior knowledge. To address this, models are typically fine-tuned using both new task data and a memory buffer of past tasks. However, CLIP's contrastive loss suffers when the memory buffer is small, leading to performance degradation on previous tasks. We propose a memory-efficient, distributionally robust method that dynamically reweights losses per class during training. Our approach, tested on class incremental settings (CIFAR-100, ImageNet1K) and a domain incremental setting (DomainNet) adapts CLIP models quickly while minimizing catastrophic forgetting, even with minimal memory usage.

### [202] [From Data Lifting to Continuous Risk Estimation: A Process-Aware Pipeline for Predictive Monitoring of Clinical Pathways](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03895)
*Pasquale Ardimento,Mario Luca Bernardi,Marta Cimitile,Samuele Latorre*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种可复现且流程感知的预测性监控管道，用于临床路径的预测分析。该方法整合了数据提升、时间重构、事件日志构建、基于前缀的表示和预测建模，支持对部分观测的患者轨迹进行持续推理。在COVID-19临床路径上以ICU入院为预测目标进行验证（4,479名患者，46,804个前缀），逻辑回归表现最优（AUC 0.906, F1 0.835），且预测性能随临床事件的积累逐步提升（AUC从早期0.642提升至后期0.942），表明医疗中的预测监控应被视作一个持续、动态感知的过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统回顾性流程挖掘无法支持对部分观测的患者轨迹进行持续推理，缺乏对临床路径进行实时预测性监控的能力，因此需要一种能够处理部分观测数据、支持渐进式风险评估的流程感知预测管道。

Method: 提出一种可复现的流程感知预测监控管道，包括数据提升（data lifting）、时间重构（temporal reconstruction）、事件日志构建、基于前缀的表示（prefix-based representation）以及预测建模。采用病例级划分（case-level split）进行训练与评估，使用4,479名患者的46,804个前缀，以ICU入院为预测目标，对比多种预测模型。

Result: 逻辑回归（Logistic Regression）表现最佳，AUC为0.906，F1-score为0.835。前缀级分析显示预测性能随临床事件积累逐步提升：AUC从早期阶段的0.642增加到后期阶段的0.942。两个关键发现：（1）预测信号沿临床路径渐进式出现；（2）流程感知表示能够从演化的患者轨迹中实现有效的早期风险估计。

Conclusion: 医疗中的预测性监控应被视作一个持续的、动态感知的过程，风险估计随着患者旅程的演化而逐步精细化，而非一次性评估。

Abstract: This paper presents a reproducible and process-aware pipeline for predictive monitoring of clinical pathways. The approach integrates data lifting, temporal reconstruction, event log construction, prefix-based representations, and predictive modeling to support continuous reasoning on partially observed patient trajectories, overcoming the limitations of traditional retrospective process mining. The framework is evaluated on COVID-19 clinical pathways using ICU admission as the prediction target, considering 4,479 patient cases and 46,804 prefixes. Predictive models are trained and evaluated using a case-level split, with 896 patients in the test set. Logistic Regression achieves the best performance (AUC 0.906, F1-score 0.835). A detailed prefix-based analysis shows that predictive performance improves progressively as new clinical events become available, with AUC increasing from 0.642 at early stages to 0.942 at later stages of the pathway. The results highlight two key findings: predictive signals emerge progressively along clinical pathways, and process-aware representations enable effective early risk estimation from evolving patient trajectories. Overall, the findings suggest that predictive monitoring in healthcare is best conceived as a continuous, dynamically aware process, in which risk estimates are progressively refined as the patient journey evolves.

### [203] [Transformers with Selective Access to Early Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03953)
*Skye Gunasekaran,Téa Wright,Rui-Jie Zhu,Jason Eshraghian*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SATFormer提出了一种上下文相关的门控机制，将早期层的值表示重用视为检索问题而非连接问题，在130M到1.3B参数规模上持续优于静态值残差和标准Transformer基线，在检索密集型任务上提升约1.5个平均点，同时保持接近基线的吞吐量和内存使用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法要么使用静态值残差（对所有token、头、上下文统一暴露第一层值投影V_1），要么使用更昂贵但更细粒度的密集/动态方法。然而，V_1的有用性并非恒定不变，不同位置可能需要不同程度的早期词汇或语义信息访问，因此需要一种自适应机制。

Method: SATFormer将早期表示重用形式化为检索问题而非连接问题，保留第一层值通路，同时通过上下文相关的门控机制控制访问。该门控能够根据token、头、上下文动态决定是否以及如何访问早期层的值表示。

Result: 在130M到1.3B参数规模的模型上，SATFormer持续改善了验证损失和零样本准确率。在检索密集型基准上，相比静态值残差方法提升了约1.5个平均点，同时吞吐量和内存使用接近标准Transformer基线。

Conclusion: 门控分析表明SATFormer学习到稀疏、深度依赖、头特定且类别敏感的访问模式，支持其学习的是选择性重用早期表示而非统一残差复制的解释。

Abstract: Several recent Transformer architectures expose later layers to representations computed in the earliest layers, motivated by the observation that low-level features can become harder to recover as the residual stream is repeatedly transformed through depth. The cheapest among these methods add static value residuals: learned mixing coefficients that expose the first-layer value projection V_1 uniformly across tokens and heads. More expressive dense or dynamic alternatives recover finer-grained access, but at higher memory cost and lower throughput. The usefulness of V_1 is unlikely to be constant across tokens, heads, and contexts; different positions plausibly require different amounts of access to early lexical or semantic information. We therefore treat early-representation reuse as a retrieval problem rather than a connectivity problem, and introduce Selective Access Transformer (SATFormer), which preserves the first-layer value pathway while controlling access with a context-dependent gate. Across models from 130M to 1.3B parameters, SATFormer consistently improves validation loss and zero-shot accuracy over the static value-residual and Transformer baselines. Its strongest gains appear on retrieval-intensive benchmarks, where it improves over static value residuals by approximately 1.5 average points, while maintaining throughput and memory usage close to the baseline Transformer. Gate analyses suggest sparse, depth-dependent, head-specific, and category-sensitive access patterns, supporting the interpretation that SATFormer learns selective reuse of early representations rather than uniform residual copying. Our code is available at https://github.com/SkyeGunasekaran/SATFormer.

</details>


### [204] [Pretrained Model Representations as Acquisition Signals for Active Learning of MLIPs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03964)
*Eszter Varga-Umbrich,Shikha Surana,Paul Duckworth,Jules Tilly,Olivier Peltre,Zachary Weller-Davies*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出直接从预训练MACE势函数的潜空间中提取两种核函数信号（神经正切核与激活核），用于主动学习中的高效采集，无需额外的不确定性头、贝叶斯训练或委员会集成。在反应性化学基准上，该方法将达到性能目标所需的数据量平均减少38%（能量误差）和28%（力误差），并证明预训练模型能诱导与模型误差对齐的潜空间几何结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 训练反应性化学的机器学习原子间势能面临量子化学标签成本高昂以及候选池中过渡态构型稀缺的瓶颈。主动学习可缓解这一问题，但其效果依赖于采集规则的设计。现有方法需要额外的不确定性头、贝叶斯训练或委员会集成，增加了复杂性。本文旨在探索是否可以直接利用预训练MLIP的潜空间信息来实现有效采集，从而消除这些额外开销。

Method: 从预训练的MACE势函数中提取两种采集信号：(1) 有限宽度神经正切核（NTK），(2) 基于隐藏潜空间特征构建的激活核。在反应性化学基准上，将这两种核函数驱动的采集策略与固定描述子基线、委员会分歧法和随机采集进行对比，评估其数据效率。

Result: 在反应性化学基准上，两种核函数方法均一致优于固定描述子基线、委员会分歧法和随机采集。达到性能目标所需数据量平均减少38%（能量误差）和28%（力误差）。预训练模型诱导的相似性空间能保留化学有意义的几何结构，并提供比随机初始化或固定描述子核更可靠的残差不确定性估计。

Conclusion: 预训练能够将潜空间几何结构与模型误差对齐，从而为反应性MLIP微调提供实用且充分的采集信号，无需额外的不确定性估计模块。

Abstract: Training machine learning interatomic potentials (MLIPs) for reactive chemistry is often bottlenecked by the high cost of quantum chemical labels and the scarcity of transition state configurations in candidate pools. Active learning (AL) can mitigate these costs, but its effectiveness hinges on the acquisition rule. We investigate whether the latent space of a pretrained MLIP already contains the information necessary for effective acquisition, eliminating the need for auxiliary uncertainty heads, Bayesian training and fine-tuning, or committee ensembles. We introduce two acquisition signals derived directly from a pretrained MACE potential: a finite-width neural tangent kernel (NTK) and an activation kernel built from hidden latent space features. On reactive-chemistry benchmarks, both kernels consistently outperform fixed-descriptor baselines, committee disagreement, and random acquisition, reducing the data required to reach performance targets by an average of 38% for energy error and 28% for force error. We further show that the pretrained model induces similarity spaces that preserve chemically meaningful structure and provide more reliable residual uncertainty estimates than randomly initialised or fixed-descriptor-based kernels. Our results suggest that pretraining aligns latent-space geometry with model error, yielding a practical and sufficient acquisition signal for reactive MLIP fine-tuning.

### [205] [A Closed-Form Adaptive-Landmark Kernel for Certified Point-Cloud and Graph Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04046)
*Sushovan Majhi,Atish Mitra,Žiga Virk,Pramita Bagchi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: PALACE 是一种数据自适应的持久性图分类引擎，基于覆盖理论核心提供了四个闭合形式保证，在多个化学图数据集上达到或超越现有方法性能，且对域膨胀具有高度鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有持久性图分析方法（如 PLACE）依赖均匀网格，对数据分布不均匀的情况效率低下。需要一种数据自适应的框架，在保持理论保证的同时提高计算效率和分类性能。

Method: 引入三个超参数（预算、半径、带宽）的交叉验证层；利用覆盖理论的 Lebesgue 数准则作为核心，推导出四个闭式保证；采用核-RKHS 分类器，结合马氏距离或各向同性替代指标进行排序选择。

Result: 在 Orbit5k 上达 91.3% 准确率（匹配 Persformer）；在 COX2 和 MUTAG 上领先所有基于图的竞争者；在 DHFR 上接近 ECP（1 pp 以内）。8 倍域膨胀下自适应放置保持 94% 准确率，而均匀网格降至 25%。

Conclusion: PALACE 是首个将覆盖理论、闭合形式保证与数据自适应相结合的可解释持久性图分类引擎，在理论和经验上均优于均匀网格方法，尤其在高维域膨胀场景下表现显著优越。

Abstract: We introduce PALACE (Persistence Adaptive-Landmark Analytic Classification Engine), the data-adaptive companion to PLACE, paying a small cross-validation tier on three knobs (budget, radii, bandwidth; $\leq 5$ choices each). A cover-theoretic core (Lebesgue-number criterion on the landmark cover) yields four closed-form guarantees. (i) A structural lower distortion bound $λ(τ;ν)$ on $\mathcal{D}_n$ under cross-diagram non-interference, with a $(D/L)^2$ budget reduction over the uniform grid when diagrams concentrate. (ii) Equal weights $w_k = K^{-1/2}$ maximizing $λ$, and farthest-point-sampling positions $2$-approximating the optimal $k$-center covering radius; both derived from training labels alone, no gradient training. (iii) A kernel-RKHS classification rate $O((k-1)\sqrt{K}/(γ\sqrt{m_{\min}}))$ with binary necessity threshold $m = Ω(\sqrt K/γ)$ from a matching Le Cam lower bound, and a closed-form filtration-selection rule. The kernel-Mahalanobis margin $\hatρ_{\mathrm{Mah}}$ is the strongest closed-form ranker across the chemical-graph pool (mean Spearman $ρ\approx +0.60$); the isotropic surrogate $\hatγ/\sqrt{K}$ admits a selection-consistency rate, and $\widehatλ$ from (i) provides an independent data-level signal (positive on COX2 and PTC). (iv) A per-prediction certificate, in non-asymptotic Pinelis and asymptotic Gaussian forms, with no calibration split. Empirically, PALACE is the strongest closed-form diagram-based method on Orbit5k ($91.3 \pm 1.0\%$, matching Persformer), leads every diagram-based competitor on COX2 and MUTAG, and is competitive on DHFR (within 1 pp of ECP). At $8\times$ domain inflation, adaptive placement maintains $94\%$ while the uniform grid collapses to chance ($25\%$ on 4-class data).

</details>
